                <div class="pop-out Op-0" style="content:;position:absolute;border-style:solid;border-top-width:0;border-bottom-width:9px;border-left-width:8px;border-right-width:8px;border-color:#e7e7e7 transparent;display:block;height:0;width:0;z-index:2147483646;top:29px;left:50%;margin-left:-8px;transition-property:opacity;transition-duration:0.1s;transition-timing-function:linear;pointer-events:none;">
                </div>

                 <div style="position:relative;background-color:white;-webkit-border-radius:5px;-moz-border-radius:5px;-khtml-border-radius:5px;border-radius:5px;border:solid 1px #e7e7e7;padding:4px;z-index:2147483645;">
                  <div style="width:47px;height:20px;">

                   </iframe>
                  </div>

               </div>
              </div>

               <div class="D-ib" style="height:40px;padding:0 11.5px;">

           <div class="Pos-r sticky-container print-article" style="min-height:315px;">
            <div class="article-inner-container" style="max-width:1280px;">
             <div class="inset-container Mx-a">
              <div class="GridTable">
               <div class="D-tbr row-template">
                <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-left">
                 <div class="content" style="width:825px;min-width:825px;">

                  </noscript>
                  <noscript>
                  </noscript>
                  <div class="GridTable grid-content">
                   <div class="D-tbr row-content">
                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-left Pend-20" style="width:305px;max-width:305px;">
                     <h1 class="Font-A-6-110 title W-100" id="article-aft-title-97498909687">
                      Go Commando or Drive a Tank with These Extreme Adventures
                     </h1>
                     <div class="attribution-component D-b W-100" id="article-aft-attribution-97498909687" style="max-width:305px;">
                      <div class="author-info author-info-text-first Pt-10 W-100 Bd-t Bd-b Bdstart-0 Bdend-0">
                       <div class="GridTable W-100">
                        <div class="D-tbr">
                         <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t">
                          <cite class="byline col D-b Fs-n" style="padding-bottom:15px;">
                           <span class="author-name Font-C-2-140 D-b">
                            <a class="attribution-name Font-C-2-140 Fw-b Whs-n" data-ylk="t1:a2;t2:article;t3:cat;t8:d2409ed9-a850-3e55-8b6f-c41e5100807e;t9:17;elm:itm;elmt:link;itc:0" href="http://www.foxnews.com/?intcmp=logo" style="color:#000;" target="_blank">
                             Fox News.com
                            </a>
                           </span>
                           <time class="date Font-C-2-140 Fw-n D-b">
                            <span>
                             September 17, 2014
                            </span>
                           </time>
                          </cite>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-right" style="max-width:500px;">
                     <div class="text-body-wrapper W-100 Font-B-1-160">
                      <noscript>
                      </noscript>
                      <div class="text-body W-100 Font-B-1-160" id="article-aft-text-body-97498909687" style="color:#222222;max-width:500px;">
                       <div class="body read-more-cut">
                        <div class="pre-cut" style="height:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;">
                         <p>
                          By Lyn Mettler
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Do you fantasize about being John Rambo or James Bond?
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Have you always wondered what it would be like to drive a tank or sneak into enemy territory with the Special Forces? These five intense experiences will let you indulge these fantasies while keeping you safely right here in reality.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           Drive a Tank
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="Go Commando or Drive a Tank with These Extreme Adventures" height="281" src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/3343f6a6901ff87928d8d486bc8789836cedc94e.jpg" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           (Courtesy:www.DriveaTank.com)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Get behind the wheel of some of Americas most fortified armored vehicles at
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:d2409ed9-a850-3e55-8b6f-c41e5100807e;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.driveatank.com/" target="_blank">
                           Drive a Tank
                          </a>
                          in Kasota, Minn. The facility has eight tanks and several military vehicles that have been used in actual combat. You can drive them in a combat scenario and run over just about anything that gets in your way. Youll receive a full safety briefing and driving tips before hopping aboard, and youll learn about the vehicles and how they are used.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Drive a tank through a wooded course with an instructor sitting shotgun, then get behind the wheel of a second tank that youll drive through a challenge course with just small vision periscopes to guide you. The best part is when you get to crush cars just like in a Monster Truck Jam. As a bonus, you can shoot historic military firearms, using up to 30 rounds, at the Drive a Tank indoor shooting range.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Cost: The cheapest package, which doesnt include crushing cars, is $399.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           Fly like Maverick and Goose
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="air combat usa" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/317cc63ed269e8d6e0ea189fdaafe065dd64b119.jpg" height="281" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           (Courtesy: Air Combat USA)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Who among us hasnt dreamed of piloting a plane Top Gun-style, Tom Cruise Ray-Bans and all? Get your fighter pilot fix at
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:d2409ed9-a850-3e55-8b6f-c41e5100807e;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://aircombat.com/%20" target="_blank">
                           Air Combat USA
                          </a>
                          , operating in 26 cities across the U.S. No experience or license is needed for your chance to spot a bogey at 3oclock and fire away in what they call the ultimate laser tag.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                            Related:
                            <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:d2409ed9-a850-3e55-8b6f-c41e5100807e;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://yhoo.it/1pglmCs" target="_blank">
                             WATCH: Anticarjacking Class? Sign Us Up! We Attend the Ultimate Driving School
                            </a>
                           </strong>
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          In this real-life experience (not a simulator), youre seated next to an instructor pilot in an SIAI Marchetti SF260, an aerobatics and military training plane that handles like an aerial version of the Ferrari, according to Air Combat USA. Take your turn outsmarting, outmaneuvering and outgunning the enemy with an air-to-air kill simulator. When you make contact (no actual guns are fired), smoke pours out of the other plane. Of course, your flight is captured on camera, so you can share your inner fighter pilot with the whole world.
                         </p>
                        </div>
                        <div class="post-cut W-100" id="post-cut" style="transition-property:none;-webkit-transition-property:none;transition-duration:10s;-webkit-transition-duration:10s;transition-timing-function:ease-in;-webkit-transition-timing-function:ease-in;overflow:hidden;max-height:0;max-width:500px;">
                         <p>
                          Cost: starting at $1,395 per person.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           Go Undercover
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="covert ops miami" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/8d340d55eac77be9162a76cf25bc246e76bcec3f.jpg" height="281" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           (Courtesy: Covert Ops Miami)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          How do elite antiterrorism units take down the enemy? You can learn firsthand on an intense two- or four-day mission with
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:d2409ed9-a850-3e55-8b6f-c41e5100807e;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.incredible-adventures.com/covert1.html" target="_blank">
                           Covert Ops Miami
                          </a>
                          as a member of an Israeli counterterrorism unit. Accompanied by Garret Machine, a native Floridian and former member of the Israeli Defense Force with a masters degree in homeland security and counterterror warfare, get ready to take down some wanted militants.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                            Related:
                            <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:d2409ed9-a850-3e55-8b6f-c41e5100807e;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://yhoo.it/1iMAprb" target="_blank">
                             The Extreme Fantasy Summer Camp Your Kids Will Love
                            </a>
                           </strong>
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <span>
                           While undercover, youll learn the Israeli martial arts technique of
                          </span>
                          <em>
                           Krav Maga
                          </em>
                          <span>
                           , go through military gas training, experience proven techniques for kidnapping militants, learn to shoot from a moving vehicle, practice counterterrorism warfare with an assault rifle, try handcuffing techniques and more.
                          </span>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Cost: Starting at $2,950 per person.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           Extreme Skydiving
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="Extreme Skydiving" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/c7e452d43955ed3471d410471d4e66ff13c85de4.jpg" height="281" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           (Courtesy:Incredible Adventures)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          If youve been there, done that when it comes to skydiving, heres a way to take it up a notch. Learn the skill of High Altitude, Low Open (HALO) parachute jumping, a technique that involves jumping from high altitudes and waiting until the last second to pull the ripcord. Our Special Forces use the technique to avoid detection. Their motto: Jump out of a perfectly good airplane at 30,000 feet because you can!
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                            Related:
                            <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:d2409ed9-a850-3e55-8b6f-c41e5100807e;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://yhoo.it/1sa8915" target="_blank">
                             Skydiving Not Extreme Enough for You? Try Rope Jumping
                            </a>
                           </strong>
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          In Somerville, Tenn., undergo training with an expert HALO jump team as part of the
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:d2409ed9-a850-3e55-8b6f-c41e5100807e;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.incredible-adventures.com/halo-jumping.html" target="_blank">
                           Tandem HALO Jumping
                          </a>
                          experience. Head up to 30,000 feet, where youll have to breathe from an oxygen mask just to keep your wits about you, and then make the leap strapped to an expert jumper. The team says it can be all said and done within just a few hours, and it recommends May through November as the best months to go.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Cost: $3,495 per person.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           Score Survival Skills
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="survival camp" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/74356813aa80328fa4aa8a8718edf36267d255b9.jpg" height="281" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           (Courtesy: Incredible Adventures)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          How would you fare on the popular TV show Naked and Afraid? Find out with TV personality Mykel Hawke, a veteran Green Beret and star of the Discovery Channel Show Man, Woman, Wild, with a weekend in the wilderness on
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:d2409ed9-a850-3e55-8b6f-c41e5100807e;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.incredible-adventures.com/specops-basic-survival.html" target="_blank">
                           Specops: Basic Survival Training
                          </a>
                          . After some classroom instruction on skills like building a fire and constructing a shelter, be ready to get dirty and hungry. Youll be given only a few select items like a canteen, compass, poncho, whistle and flashlight, and then youll be sent out into the wild to locate food and water and spend the night alone. And dont try to sneak in your cellphone; theyll take it from you when training begins.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Cost: $1,000 per person.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           More from Fox News.com
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>

                           Would you spend a night in this ocean cliff villa?
                          </a>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:d2409ed9-a850-3e55-8b6f-c41e5100807e;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.foxnews.com/travel/2014/09/09/legoland-leads-host-new-theme-parks-coming-to-dubai/" target="_blank">
                           <span>
                            Legoland leads a host of new theme parks coming to Dubai
                           </span>
                          </a>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:d2409ed9-a850-3e55-8b6f-c41e5100807e;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.foxnews.com/travel/2014/09/09/take-walk-in-clouds-on-new-suspension-bridge-between-mountain-peaks/%20%20" target="_blank">
                           <span>
                            Take a walk in the clouds on new suspension bridge between mountain peaks
                           </span>
                          </a>
                         </p>
                         <p>

world\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E), even though its rare for visitors to actually catch a glimpse of the big, spotted cats. These trails lead to several \u003Cspan style=\"color: blue;\"\u003Ewaterfalls\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E as well as the summit of Victoria Peak, the highest peak in Belize. Skyscanner survey\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;found that&#xA0;only one percent of people actually prefer the middle seat on a plane. No surprise there. But Frontier Airlines may change all that.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe budget airline plans to stop the middle seat haters with its new 19-inch middle seats, according to \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.cntraveler.com\u002Fstories\u002F2015-07-09\u002Fthe-one-airline-that-s-actually-improving-the-middle-seat\"\u003Ecntraveler.com\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. That size is one inch wider than Frontier&#x2019;s window and aisle seats and, the airline claims, wider than on any other U.S. airline.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAnother bonus? Frontier does not plan to charge more for the wider middle seats.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ESound too good to be true? It&#x2019;s not: There are downsides. The seats will have less padding; passengers in these seats will be closer to the seat in front of them and behind them (less pitch), which affects legroom; and the seats do not recline (though Frontier calls them&#xA0;&#x201C;pre-reclined&#x201D;).&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETo avoid all these pitfalls, a traveler would still have to purchase&#xA0;a middle seat in the more expensive premium economy &#x201C;Stretch&#x201D; section.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fthe-new-airline-seat-that-turns-economy-into-business-101370413642.html\"\u003EThe New Airline Seat That Turns Economy Into Business Class\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EPerhaps the inch of extra room in the middle seat is to offset some of the other changes coming to Frontier. According to cntraveler.com, this year the airline is adding 12 seats to every Airbus A320 and A319 it flies. It&#x2019;s also set to be the first U.S. airline to put a 186-seat A320 into service, which has an extra six seats, thanks to smaller bathrooms.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBut Frontier isn&#x2019;t worried about that:&#xA0;&quot;Customers fly on regional aircraft all the time when they can&#x2019;t stand up in the lavatory,&#x201C;says Daniel Shurz, chief commercial officer for Frontier. &quot;They handle that just fine.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWATCH: Flying Singapore Airlines in First Class for an Hour Ruined My Life\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Ciframe width=\"540\" height=\"303\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fscreen.yahoo.com\u002Fa-broad-abroad\u002Ffirst-class-broad-abroad-181008113.html?format=embed\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fiframe\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day. Greenlands Finest Microbrew Beers","summary":"I'm a beer woman. So on my trip to Greenland, when I heard there was a craft brewery in town, I made a beeline for it.","body":"\u003Cp\u003EAnybody who knows me knows I don&#x2019;t drink vodka. I don&#x2019;t do tequila. And I&#x2019;ve never been a big fan of anything that comes with a garnish. I am, however, a beer girl. Raised in Cincinnati, a town with German roots, I have a deep love of hops, and over the years my tastes have been refined from \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fhudepohlbeer.com\u002F\"\u003EHudepohl\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and Schlitz to craft beers. Don&#x2019;t get me wrong &#x2014; when stuck on a riverboat for a bachelorette party in, say, Austin, Texas (thanks to my sister Emily), I will still happily down a Bud, a Coors, or a Schlitz. But I have learned to appreciate the fine craft of beer making and love a small-batch brew. So on my trip to Greenland, when I heard there was a craft brewery in town, I made a beeline for it.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Ffinger-pulling-head-pulling-and-kick-the-seal-122521580652.html\"\u003EFinger Pulling and Kick the Seal &#x2014; Welcome to the Arctic Games!\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F93fb6d09ed4cf36c50b1cd8100b9a9da95be5f9d.png\" alt=\"Taste-Testing Greenland&#x2019;s Finest Microbrew Beers\" width=\"540\" height=\"304\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThe Godthaab Bryghus brewery is in a building that conveniently also houses a dive bar called Daddy&#x2019;s. While &#x201C;Daddy&#x201D; is a great guy named Gert, the actual brewery is run by Mikael Sorenson, who swears that the beer there is made with glacier ice that is at least 2,000 years old.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;Yes, we have men who go out onto the ice and cut slabs off the glaciers for us and bring them back here for our beer,&#x201D; Sorenson said.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E[Side note: Apparently ice cutting is a big business. Down the street is an ice cream shop that also uses 2,000-year-old ice. &#x201C;Ice cream in Greenland?&#x201D; you may be asking. &#x201C;Isn&#x2019;t it cold enough?&#x201D; No. It&#x2019;s not. Greenland has the second largest ice cream consumption per capita in the world, second only to Finland. Go figure.]\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"304\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F3a590de53797cb2f646953e3212a190735cb2dff.png\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EWhile there are no official stats on how much beer is consumed in &#xA0;Nuuk, Greenland&#x2019;s capital, judging by the crowds in the bars and the continual snow, I&#x2019;d say it ranks right up there. And frankly, I can&#x2019;t say I blame them &#x2014; the weather is rough (see previous episode: &#x201C;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fsnowmageddon-2015-cabin-fever-hits-hard-in-123462240287.html\"\u003ESnowmageddon 2015: Cabin Fever Hits Hard in Greenland\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#x201D;), and the beer is delicious. At the time I visited, there were five beers on tap, including the Musk Ox, the Eric the Red, and the Polar Bear (they like to name the beers after local animals). And here&#x2019;s a tip: While they are all delicious, if you ever find yourself at Daddy&#x2019;s in Nuuk, ask for Gert and Mikael and get them to give you the unfiltered versions of all the beers. They may smell like dirty feet, but they taste like heaven.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fsnowmageddon-2015-cabin-fever-hits-hard-in-123462240287.html\"\u003ESnowmageddon 2015: Cabin Fever Hits Hard in Greenland\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThere is only one problem with the Godthaab Bryghus beer &#x2014; while it is possibly the best beer I have ever tasted (and trust: I have tasted a lot of beer), they don&#x2019;t export. So to get 2,000-year-old glacier-water beer, you have to go to the source. It&#x2019;s worth it. \u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cb\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day. 000","data_version":"1","title":"Go These five intense experiences will let you indulge these fantasies while keeping you safely right here in reality.","body":"\u003Cp\u003EBy Lyn Mettler\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EDo you fantasize about being John Rambo or James Bond?\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EHave you always wondered what it would be like to drive a tank or sneak into enemy territory with the Special Forces? These five intense experiences will let you indulge these fantasies while keeping you safely right here in reality.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EDrive a Tank\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cimg alt=\"Go Commando or Drive a Tank with These Extreme Adventures\" src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w500\u002F3343f6a6901ff87928d8d486bc8789836cedc94e.jpg\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cem\u003E(Courtesy:&#xA0;www.DriveaTank.com)\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EGet behind the wheel of some of America&#x2019;s most fortified armored vehicles at \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.driveatank.com\u002F\"\u003EDrive a Tank\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;in Kasota, Minn. The facility has eight tanks and several military vehicles that have been used in actual combat. You can drive them in a combat scenario and run over just about anything that gets in your way. You&#x2019;ll receive a full safety briefing and driving tips before hopping aboard, and you&#x2019;ll learn about the vehicles and how they are used.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EDrive a tank through a wooded course with an instructor sitting shotgun, then get behind the wheel of a second tank that you&#x2019;ll drive through a challenge course with just small vision periscopes to guide you. The best part is when you get to crush cars just like in a Monster Truck Jam. As a bonus, you can shoot historic military firearms, using up to 30 rounds, at the Drive a Tank indoor shooting range.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ECost: The cheapest package, which doesn&#x2019;t include crushing cars, is $399.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EFly like Maverick and Goose\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cimg alt=\"air combat usa\" src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w500\u002F317cc63ed269e8d6e0ea189fdaafe065dd64b119.jpg\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cem\u003E(Courtesy: Air Combat USA)\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EWho among us hasn&#x2019;t dreamed of piloting a plane &#x201C;Top Gun&#x201D;-style, Tom Cruise Ray-Bans and all? Get your fighter pilot fix at \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Faircombat.com\u002F%20\"\u003EAir Combat USA\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, operating in 26 cities across the U.S. No experience or license is needed for your chance to spot a bogey at 3&#xA0;o&#x2019;clock and fire away in what they call the &#x201C;ultimate laser tag.&#x201D;&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cem\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fyhoo.it\u002F1pglmCs\"\u003EWATCH: Anticarjacking Class? Sign Us Up! We Attend the Ultimate Driving School\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EIn this real-life experience (not a simulator), you&#x2019;re seated next to an instructor pilot in an SIAI Marchetti SF260, an aerobatics and military training plane that handles like an aerial version of the Ferrari, according to Air Combat USA. Take your turn outsmarting, outmaneuvering and outgunning the enemy with an air-to-air &#x201C;kill&#x201D; simulator. When you make contact (no actual guns are fired), smoke pours out of the other plane. Of course, your flight is captured on camera, so you can share your inner fighter pilot with the whole world.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ECost: starting at $1,395 per person.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EGo Undercover\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cimg alt=\"covert ops miami\" src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w500\u002F8d340d55eac77be9162a76cf25bc246e76bcec3f.jpg\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cem\u003E(Courtesy: Covert Ops Miami)\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EHow do elite antiterrorism units take down the enemy? You can learn firsthand on an intense two- or four-day mission with \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.incredible-adventures.com\u002Fcovert1.html\"\u003ECovert Ops Miami\u003C\u002Fa\u003E as a member of an Israeli counterterrorism unit. Accompanied by Garret Machine, a native Floridian and former member of the Israeli Defense Force with a master&#x2019;s degree in homeland security and counterterror warfare, get ready to take down some wanted militants.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cem\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003ERelated:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fyhoo.it\u002F1iMAprb\"\u003EThe Extreme Fantasy Summer Camp Your Kids Will Love\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan\u003EWhile undercover, you&#x2019;ll learn the Israeli martial arts technique of \u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003Cem\u003EKrav Maga\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003Cspan\u003E, go through military gas training, experience proven techniques for kidnapping militants, learn to shoot from a moving vehicle, practice counterterrorism warfare with an assault rifle, try handcuffing techniques and more.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ECost: Starting at $2,950 per person.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EExtreme Skydiving\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cimg alt=\"Extreme Skydiving\" src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w500\u002Fc7e452d43955ed3471d410471d4e66ff13c85de4.jpg\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cem\u003E(Courtesy:&#xA0;Incredible Adventures)\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EIf you&#x2019;ve been there, done that when it comes to skydiving, here&#x2019;s a way to take it up a notch. Learn the skill of High Altitude, Low Open (HALO) parachute jumping, a technique that involves jumping from high altitudes and waiting until the last second to pull the ripcord. Our Special Forces use the technique to avoid detection. Their motto: &#x201C;Jump out of a perfectly good airplane at 30,000 feet because you can!&#x201D;&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cem\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003E&#xA0;Related: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fyhoo.it\u002F1sa8915\"\u003ESkydiving Not Extreme Enough for You? Try Rope Jumping\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EIn Somerville, Tenn., undergo training with an expert HALO jump team as part of the \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.incredible-adventures.com\u002Fhalo-jumping.html\"\u003ETandem HALO Jumping\u003C\u002Fa\u003E experience. Head up to 30,000 feet, where you&#x2019;ll have to breathe from an oxygen mask just to keep your wits about you, and then make the leap strapped to an expert jumper. The team says it can be all said and done within just a few hours, and it recommends May through November as the best months to go.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ECost: $3,495 per person.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EScore Survival Skills\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cimg alt=\"survival camp\" src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w500\u002F74356813aa80328fa4aa8a8718edf36267d255b9.jpg\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cem\u003E(Courtesy: Incredible Adventures)\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EHow would you fare on the popular TV show &#x201C;Naked and Afraid&#x201D;? Find out with TV personality Mykel Hawke, a veteran Green Beret and star of the Discovery Channel Show &#x201C;Man, Woman, Wild,&#x201D; with a weekend in the wilderness on \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.incredible-adventures.com\u002Fspecops-basic-survival.html\"\u003ESpecops: Basic Survival Training\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. After some classroom instruction on skills like building a fire and constructing a shelter, be ready to get dirty and hungry. You&#x2019;ll be given only a few select items like a canteen, compass, poncho, whistle and flashlight, and then you&#x2019;ll be sent out into the wild to locate food and water and spend the night alone. And don&#x2019;t try to sneak in your cellphone; they&#x2019;ll take it from you when training begins.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ECost: $1,000 per person.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EMore from Fox News.com\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.foxnews.com\u002Ftravel\u002F2014\u002F09\u002F09\u002Fwould-spend-night-or-two-in-this-vertical-villa\u002F\"\u003EWould you spend a night in this ocean cliff villa?\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.foxnews.com\u002Ftravel\u002F2014\u002F09\u002F09\u002Flegoland-leads-host-new-theme-parks-coming-to-dubai\u002F\"\u003E\u003Cspan\u003ELegoland leads a host of new theme parks coming to Dubai\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.foxnews.com\u002Ftravel\u002F2014\u002F09\u002F09\u002Ftake-walk-in-clouds-on-new-suspension-bridge-between-mountain-peaks\u002F%20%20\"\u003E\u003Cspan\u003ETake a walk in the clouds on new suspension bridge between mountain peaks\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day.
